# And there we are, the 300th regular enemy! :)
# This 300th enemy also happens to be the first depth 50 enemy in the game. Because of this,
# we need to make a special monster to commemorate this event!

# Enters the Phoenix sub-family of bird monsters.
# This legendary bird of fire is said to be able to revive from it's ashes. And here,
# the legend is quite true.

# There are many kinds of Phoenix. The first one is the Phoenix of Solar Flames.
# This is a very powerful enemy that will require quite a bit of efforts to defeat.
# Fire fields, powerful attacks, very fast, very strong, high in every areas... your
# best hope lies in a powerful Cold or Water attack. And actually, it's the only thing
# that can actually KILL it for good!

# Good luck! :)

D:crystalline in nature as opposed to true bird-like feathers, but that doesn't seem to affect 
D:the creature's flight. The scales on it's tail are made of what seems to be diamonds.

###### SCALED MONSTERS ######

# Leveling up is not the key. These monsters will ALWAYS be a challenge! A good character build,
# powerful fully leveled items, and a well executed strategy are required to win.
# The signature monster type of Secret Levels! :)

# The depth level of the monsters are equal to the player's level, unless the player is below
# their base depth level.

# The hp roll is the hp roll per depth levels. So if you give 2d2, and the monster becomes depth
# 20, hp roll will be 40d40.

# Base stats, skills and base AC are all percentile values of the depth level. So if you make
# a monster's stats 100, skills 20 and AC 1000, at level 20, it will have base stats of 20, skills
# of 4 and base AC of 200.

# Dices rolls of attacks and spells powers are also percentile value of depth level.

# The non-scaled values are speed, blows and number of spells.

#############################
